msg:This time I booked an executive sea view king room. I asked in advance if the view of the king bed was better than the twin beds. As a result, I didn't get back from Gulangyu until almost eleven o'clock that day (I couldn't get a taxi after getting off the boat. There was a traffic jam near the hotel and many drivers were unwilling to come. In the end, I rode a shared bicycle to get back to the hotel. There were no bicycle lanes in many places, which was a bit dangerous. I had to ride to the parking spot near the Xiamen University Medical College 200 meters away).

The room was very good and the facilities were great. As soon as I entered the door, there were little bears + love balloons + fruits, which was very ceremonial; the coffee capsules had a dark chocolate flavor, which I liked very much; the tea was also pure tea, Dahongpao and green tea. The bathroom was my favorite. The water was super big, and the two shower heads sprayed together. It was so enjoyable! Bairuide washing and care, the taste of wilderness lonely soul, the big bottle was very sufficient, and the moisturizer was very relaxing. I didn't have time to soak in the bathtub this time, I was playing outside every day. The bed was also very comfortable to sleep in and cleaned.

I didn't get any executive trea**ent. I went to the 54th floor yesterday when it was cloudy but didn't see the sunset. There wasn't much food for dinner (very little), but the curry tasted good. However, Yuna from the Executive Lounge at Conrad Xiamen was super good. She served tea to the children, asked them considerately, and reminded them when they could have afternoon tea (although they missed it because of the schedule). She also gave them tangerine peel and red bean paste, which the children liked very much. The overall experience was very good!

It rained last night, and it was cloudy this morning. Then suddenly there was a sea of ‚Äã‚Äãclouds, and then the clouds and mist dissipated a little, and the sea was colorful, like a fairyland.

Shapowei is downstairs, and there are many snacks; it's not congested to take a taxi to the Zhenhai Road subway station; it's inconvenient to take a taxi to the scenic spot when there are many people, so you can share a bicycle to get in and out, or walk to experience it.

It will be the first choice for accommodation in Xiamen, highly recommended!

msg:It was my first time to Xiamen. I read a lot of guides, and there were many good and bad reviews. But I finally chose Conrad Hotel, purely for leisure and vacation. Even on rainy days, I can lie down and enjoy the scenery. This time I booked an executive room. I took a 6-hour high-speed train from Shanghai and arrived at the hotel at 19:30 on the evening of 5/1. Edison at the front desk was very enthusiastic and gave children breakfast and Conrad bears. The children were in a good mood and their fatigue disappeared. We stayed in the room on the 52nd floor. The floor was high enough and the view was good enough. We walked in the city during the day and returned to the room at night to make a cup of coffee and sit in the bathtub to soak our feet, watching TV and enjoying the night view. It was wonderful. In addition to the unbeatable sea view, Conrad also has an excellent location. It is convenient for traveling with children. It is next to Shimao Mall and there is a Lawson supermarket downstairs. The back door of the hotel leads directly to the viewing platform. It takes only 15 minutes to walk to Xiamen University. A wonderful day starts with breakfast while enjoying the sea view. Breakfast is served in the buffet restaurant on the 38th floor. There are many varieties of food, and you can eat until you are full every day. My favorite is the chewy fish balls, which are a must-order for every meal. They are paired with shacha noodles and bone soup, each with its own flavor. During the May Day holiday, I booked a buffet dinner. The steak was of good quality and worth trying. Goodnight snacks were delivered to the room every night. On the first day, it was peanut soup, on the second day, it was tangerine peel and red bean soup, and on the third day, it was wolfberry and white fungus soup. Before leaving, I wanted to buy some specialties, so I went to Huang Yuantang on the first floor of the hotel to purchase and express them directly back, which was very convenient. This trip to Xiamen was perfect because of the blessing of Conrad, and I look forward to the next time.

When I checked in, the Xiamen Marathon was running, and I could see the marathon below from the room. I have to say that this feeling is really good.

When I checked out from Langham Place, it was 12:30 noon. I didn't expect that the hotel had arranged a room in advance and I could check in directly. This is very efficient. Check-in is on the 38th floor, and there will be someone in charge of arranging the luggage in the lobby on the first floor.

The deluxe executive sea view room includes breakfast, afternoon tea and dinner. Three meals a day can be settled in the hotel. The room is arranged on the top floor of the 53rd floor. The view is super good no matter it is day or night. You can overlook the beautiful scenery of Gulangyu Island every time you reach the sunset west When you are down, the situation makes you completely reluctant to step out of the hotel, and you just want to let the beautiful scenery stay at this moment forever.

Xiamen Conrad opened in 2016. Compared with Waldorf Astoria, a high-end brand owned by Hilton, the room decoration design is definitely not so new and fashionable, but it is worth staying once for the only invincible high-altitude sea view in Xiamen. My favorite is the big bathtub by the window where you can enjoy the sea view while soaking in the bath. There is also a small TV in the bathtub, so you can watch the World Cup while soaking in the bath at night. In addition to the traditional bathrobe, Xiamen Conrad also has a red bathrobe, which girls should like, and it looks good in photos. The toiletries are in large bottles of environmentally friendly packaging Byredo and cannot be taken away, which is a pity.

Due to the reason of YQ, the executive lounge is changed to the full-time restaurant at Pier 38 on the 38th floor of the hotel. The afternoon tea and dinner are all set menus. It's a pity that there is no wine, only fruit juice. The buffet breakfast can be eaten facing the sea. Several western pastries are delicious, and the fatigue of the journey is also swept away.

Since I was playing outside all day, I didn't have time to go to the swimming pool. It is said that the hotel swimming pool has an invincible high-altitude view, but I missed it. When I returned to the hotel in the evening, I found that the accompanying gift was a box of Su Xiaotang gift box, which contained Xiamen‚Äôs special snacks. Overall, it was a very pleasant stay experience. I charged a doctor bear and a bathrobe bear perfectly.

Move, wait for us to ask), go to the 38th floor to check in, go to the room is another elevator, from the underground garage to the room, you need to change three elevators! Is this a brainless design? I think it's not easy for everyone, but this time I can't help but give bad reviews. msg:Experience Xiamen 54th Floor Sea View Hotel, come to Conrad

The location is good. It is very close to Xiamen University, Shapowei, Yanwu Bridge and the viewing platform. There are shopping and eating around. It is also close to the place where nucleic acid is made.

The hotel in 2016 has been maintained for 6 years and the facilities are still relatively new. The sea view of the floor-to-ceiling windows in the lobby on the 38th floor is indeed more eye-catching. The front desk service is very good, and the experience ambassador Carol is also arranged to consult the housekeeper if you have anything to do, including ordering meals, etc. can be arranged in advance. Hilton Group's overall service is still in place.

The room is quite big, but the decoration is really not so trendy. Compared with the newly opened hotel, it is slightly old-fashioned. Good weather is coming.
The toiletries are Byredo, a brand in Stockholm, Sweden, which tastes very good. I like to buy a bottle home.
There are also complimentary refreshments, fruit bowls and soft drinks from the minibar.
The bedding is very comfortable. I am very picky about pillows because of the bad cervical vertebrae.
 
The gym and swimming pool are on the 37th floor and there is no view. It should work well on sunny days. There are not many people, and the feeling of enjoying the swimming pool by yourself is really not too good.

I ate two meals at the Chinese restaurant and liked it very much. It really is the restaurant of the year. Quality is good. The frozen bamboo shoots are delicious.

There are many varieties of breakfast restaurants, and the sight line is also good. The sand tea noodles taste good, my friends want to try it.


Disadvantages: the air conditioner is too loud, the kettle takes too long to boil water, the plugboards on the workbench are in a mess, and there is no place to plug in the power of the computer. I hope this can be improved.

msg:This time I came to Xiamen to check on the Internet for a long time, and finally chose the Conrad Hotel. The check-in experience was really satisfactory.
Conrad Hotel may be the best hotel in Xiamen to enjoy the sea view. All rooms in the hotel are above the 40th floor. The sea view room we stayed in can directly watch Gulangyu Island, Xiamen Port and Xiamen Bay in the room. Here, the sunrise and sunset of Xiamen Bay and the ebb and flow of the tide can be seen, even if you sit by the window in a daze all day, it is a kind of enjoyment. A few tens of meters downstairs from the hotel is the free and open sea viewing platform of Yanwu Bridge. There is also a sandy beach below the platform. It is also very convenient to watch the sea at close range. There is a shopping mall next to the hotel, which is convenient for shopping; you can walk one or two hundred meters to the Shapowei Art District in Xiamen, where there are many snack food stalls, literary and retro shops.
The hotel rooms are very comfortable, all rooms are more than 50 square meters in size, more than the average luxury hotel. The open design of the room and the high floor height combined with the wide and endless sea view make people feel comfortable as soon as they enter. In addition to the sea view from the bedroom, you can also enjoy the sea view while bathing in the bathroom. Some details also make people feel the originality of the hotel, such as the smart toilet that has been warmed up before the guest enters the room, the retro-style capsule coffee machine cleverly integrated into the room design style, the air-conditioning controlled separately in the bathroom and the bedroom, and the TV embedded in front of the bathtub. , The bedside design is ingeniously suitable for a small desk lamp that can be turned on blindly (which can be used as a night light) and so on. The soundproofing effect of the room is also very good. We have other guests staying next door, but there is no noise at all during the few days of staying.
The hotel‚Äôs service is also impressive. All the staff are very enthusiastic and the service is in place. The buckwheat neck pillow we needed was quickly prepared for us and it was very comfortable. Special thanks to the hotel manager Hu, who contacted me in advance to confirm the check-in time and gave us the daily breakfast.
In short, next time I come to Xiamen, I will definitely live in Conrad
